      // Apply theme immediately to prevent flash
      (function () {
        function applyTheme() {
          const stored = localStorage.getItem('theme');
          const systemTheme = window.matchMedia?.(
            '(prefers-color-scheme: dark)',
          ).matches
            ? 'dark'
            : 'light';
          const theme = stored ?? systemTheme;

          // Always explicitly set the theme state
          if (theme === 'dark') {
            document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
          } else {
            document.documentElement.classList.remove('dark');
          }
        }

        // Apply theme on initial load
        applyTheme();

        // Apply theme after Astro page swap (View Transitions)
        document.addEventListener('astro:after-swap', applyTheme);
      })();

fill="currentFill"></path> </svg> <span class="sr-only">Loading...</span> </div> <script>
  document.addEventListener('astro:before-preparation', event => {
    const originalLoader = event.loader;
    event.loader = async function () {
      const spinner = document.getElementById('page-transition-spinner');
      // If it takes more than 0.5s to load, show the spinner
      const h1 = document.getElementsByTagName('h1');
      const main = document.getElementsByTagName('main');
      const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
        spinner?.classList.remove('opacity-0');
        h1[0]?.classList.add('animate-pulse');
        main[0]?.classList.add('animate-pulse');
        spinner?.classList.remove('opacity-0');
      }, 500);
      await originalLoader();
      clearTimeout(timeout);
      spinner?.classList.add('opacity-0');
    };
  });
</script> <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://img.ly/static/imgly-website-components/imgly-website-components.css" as="style"><noscript><link rel="stylesheet" href="https://img.ly/static/imgly-website-components/imgly-website-components.css"></noscript><div id="imgly-website-components-cookies"></div><script>

            const el = document.getElementById(id);

          };
          mount('imgly-website-components-cookies', Cookies, {
            plausibleSettings: { props: { source: 'documentation' } },

<p>Base64 encoding transforms binary image data into ASCII text, enabling you to embed images directly in HTML, store them in text-only databases, or transmit them through JSON APIs without binary handling.</p>

<h2 id="export-a-block-to-base64">Export a Block to Base64<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#export-a-block-to-base64">#</a></h2>
<p>Use <code>engine.block.export()</code> to export a design block as a Blob, then convert it to a Base64 data URI.</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">const</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#006BB8;--1:#9CDCFE">currentPage</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">engine</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">scene</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">getCurrentPage</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">()</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">!</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">;</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">const</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#006BB8;--1:#9CDCFE">blob</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#AC00D8;--1:#C586C0">await</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">engine</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">block</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">export</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">currentPage</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, {</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">  </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">mimeType:</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;image/png&#39;</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">});</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">const</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#006BB8;--1:#9CDCFE">base64</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#AC00D8;--1:#C586C0">await</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">blobToBase64</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">blob</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="const currentPage = engine.scene.getCurrentPage()!;const blob = await engine.block.export(currentPage, {  mimeType: 'image/png'});const base64 = await blobToBase64(blob);"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<p>The export returns a Blob containing the rendered image. You then convert this Blob to a Base64 data URI using the browser’s <code>FileReader</code> API. The resulting string includes the MIME type prefix (<code>data:image/png;base64,...</code>), making it ready for immediate use as an image source.</p>
<h2 id="convert-blob-to-base64">Convert Blob to Base64<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#convert-blob-to-base64">#</a></h2>
<p>Convert the exported Blob into a Base64 data URI using the browser’s <code>FileReader</code> API.</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">private</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">blobToBase64</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">blob</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">: </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">Blob</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">): </span><span style="--0:#227188;--1:#4EC9B0">Promise</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">&lt;</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">string</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">&gt;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> {</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent"><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">  </span></span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">return new </span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">Promise</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">((</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">resolve</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">reject</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">) </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">=&gt;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> {</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">    </span><span style="--0:#227188;--1:#4EC9B0">const</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">reader</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">new</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">FileReader</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">();</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">    </span><span style="--0:#227188;--1:#4EC9B0">reader</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">onloadend</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> () </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">=&gt;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">resolve</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">reader</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">result</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#AC00D8;--1:#C586C0">as</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#227188;--1:#4EC9B0">string</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">    </span><span style="--0:#227188;--1:#4EC9B0">reader</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">onerror</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> () </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">=&gt;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">reject</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">reader</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">error</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">    </span><span style="--0:#227188;--1:#4EC9B0">reader</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#227188;--1:#4EC9B0">readAsDataURL</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#227188;--1:#4EC9B0">blob</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent"><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">  </span></span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">});</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">}</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="private blobToBase64(blob: Blob): Promise<string> {  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {    const reader = new FileReader();    reader.onloadend = () => resolve(reader.result as string);    reader.onerror = () => reject(reader.error);    reader.readAsDataURL(blob);  });}"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<p>The <code>readAsDataURL()</code> method returns a complete data URI including the MIME type prefix (<code>data:image/png;base64,...</code>). This wrapper converts the callback-based FileReader into a Promise for cleaner async/await usage.</p>
<h2 id="customize-the-built-in-export-action">Customize the Built-in Export Action<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#customize-the-built-in-export-action">#</a></h2>
<p>Override the default <code>exportDesign</code> action to integrate Base64 conversion into CE.SDK’s built-in export flow.</p>
<div class="expressive-code"><figure class="frame"><figcaption class="header"></figcaption><pre data-language="typescript"><code><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">actions</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">register</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;exportDesign&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">async</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> () </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">=&gt;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> {</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">  </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">const</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#006BB8;--1:#9CDCFE">currentPage</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">engine</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">scene</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">getCurrentPage</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">()</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">!</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">;</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">  </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">const</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#006BB8;--1:#9CDCFE">blob</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#AC00D8;--1:#C586C0">await</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">engine</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">block</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">export</span><span class="indent">    </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">mimeType:</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;image/png&#39;</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent"><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">  </span></span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">});</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">  </span><span style="--0:#0000FF;--1:#599ED7">const</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#006BB8;--1:#9CDCFE">base64</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span class="indent">  </span><span style="--0:#AC00D8;--1:#C586C0">await</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6"> </span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">cesdk</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">utils</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">.</span><span style="--0:#795E26;--1:#DCDCAA">downloadFile</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">(</span><span style="--0:#001080;--1:#9CDCFE">blob</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">, </span><span style="--0:#A31515;--1:#CE9178">&#39;image/png&#39;</span><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">);</span></div></div><div class="ec-line"><div class="code"><span style="--0:#000000;--1:#E6E6E6">});</span></div></div></code></pre><div class="copy"><div aria-live="polite"></div><button title="Copy to clipboard" data-copied="Copied!" data-code="cesdk.actions.register('exportDesign', async () => {  const currentPage = engine.scene.getCurrentPage()!;  const blob = await engine.block.export(currentPage, {    mimeType: 'image/png'  });  const base64 = await this.blobToBase64(blob);  await cesdk.utils.downloadFile(blob, 'image/png');});"><div></div></button></div></figure></div>
<p>When registered, this action replaces the default export behavior. Any UI component or keyboard shortcut that triggers <code>exportDesign</code> will use your custom handler instead.</p>
<h2 id="download-the-export">Download the Export<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#download-the-export">#</a></h2>
<p>Use <code>cesdk.utils.downloadFile()</code> to save the exported Blob to the user’s device. The method accepts a Blob and MIME type, triggering a browser download with the appropriate file extension.</p>
<h2 id="when-to-use-base64">When to Use Base64<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#when-to-use-base64">#</a></h2>
<p>Base64 encoding works well for:</p>
<ul>
<li>Embedding images directly in HTML or CSS without additional HTTP requests</li>
<li>Storing images in text-only databases like Redis or localStorage</li>
<li>Transmitting images through JSON APIs that don’t support binary data</li>
<li>Generating data URIs for email templates</li>
</ul>
<aside class="prose-p:m-0 prose-h2:m-0 prose-h3:m-0 mb-8 rounded-lg border px-6 py-4 text-sm bg-imglygray-200 dark:bg-imglygray-900 border-imglygray-600 dark:border-dark-imglygray-300 dark:text-imglygray-300 text-imglygray-900 border-imglygray-600 "> <p>Base64 increases file size by approximately 33%. For images larger than 100KB, consider binary storage or direct URL references instead.</p> </aside>
<h2 id="troubleshooting">Troubleshooting<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#troubleshooting">#</a></h2>
<p><strong>Base64 string too long</strong> — Use JPEG or WebP formats with lower quality settings. Reduce dimensions with <code>targetWidth</code> and <code>targetHeight</code> export options.</p>
<p><strong>Image not displaying</strong> — Verify the data URI includes the correct MIME type prefix. Check that the string wasn’t truncated during storage or transmission.</p>
<p><strong>Performance issues</strong> — FileReader operations are asynchronous but encoding large images can still block the UI. Consider Web Workers for images over 1MB.</p>
<h2 id="api-reference">API Reference<a class="anchor-link" aria-label="Permalink to section" href="#api-reference">#</a></h2>

































<table><thead><tr><th>Method</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>engine.block.export(block, options)</code></td><td>Export a block to a Blob with format options (<code>mimeType</code>, <code>jpegQuality</code>, <code>webpQuality</code>, <code>targetWidth</code>, <code>targetHeight</code>)</td></tr><tr><td><code>engine.scene.getCurrentPage()</code></td><td>Get the currently active page block</td></tr><tr><td><code>FileReader.readAsDataURL(blob)</code></td><td>Convert Blob to Base64 data URI (Browser API)</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.utils.downloadFile(blob, mimeType)</code></td><td>Download a Blob as a file</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.actions.register(name, handler)</code></td><td>Register or override an action</td></tr><tr><td><code>cesdk.ui.showNotification(options)</code></td><td>Display a notification to the user</td></tr></tbody></table>
